maśānti mwang mangastuti*

ri tĕlas watĕk dewatā,
mantuk ring swarga lālana,
rĕp hyang Wiṣṇu muwah Krĕṣṇa,
somyâpañ citta nirmala*

sang hyang Śakra wawang malwī,
mare śrī Krĕṣṇa harṣaja,
munggwing wāhana mātangga,
iniring ning warāpsara*

wawang mojar sirânāntwa,
he sang nātha lihat prabhu,
bhārā don mami yan prāpta,
mawehânugrahê kita*

nān ling sang hyang Śakra mojar,
narendrâtyantêng garjita,
dewanātha mahādibya,
sanmatâsiha ri nghulun*

nihan tânugraha sang hyang,
ri nghulun tulusâsiha,
sang watĕk ratu sang hantu,
kapwa wehĕnta jīwita*

narendra Druma kasyasih,
pĕjah mwang putra ring raṇa,
amet śaraṇa tan polih,
yângde mār i twas i nghulun*

Yadu-Wrĕsṇy-Andhakâdinya,
lāwan sang pininang māti,
sāmānta pratisāmānta,
huripĕn de sureśwara*

bhrĕtya putra kadang warga,
sang watĕk ratu kāsihan,
pĕjah tan tĕkan ing mrĕtyu,
yatikā huripĕn muwah*

Cedi Karṇa Jarāsandha,
byaktêki n musuh i nghulun,
tathāpi huripĕn sang hyang,
towin kadang ikā tĕhĕr*

paritrāṇâkrĕtadharma,
winiśeṣa ri sang prabhu,
śatru towin paritrāṇan,
marapwan mari durjana*

ya tā ling śrī mahārāja,
sumahur hyang surapati,
prabhu toh haywa sandeha,
astu kahyunta dadyā ya*

sampun mojar bhaṭārendra,
rĕp dhyāyī sira niścala,
tĕkâng amrĕta ring kuṇḍi,
paniram nira ring pĕjah*

tan asowe dahat sang hyang,
mahurip sang watĕk ratu,
tĕka ring śatru sing yogya,
labdhajīwa tĕkeng bala*

<Jagaddhita>:112.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ – | ⏑ ⏓

warṇan tôlah i sang watĕk ratu samâhurip agarawalan sirâwungū,
ndā tapwan matutur dahat warurutĕn tĕhĕr angusap-usap matâpĕḍe,
kāścaryan mulati ng pĕjah rudhirasāgara giri śawa ning gajah kuda,
nāhan hetu nira n saniścaya ri paprang ira paḍa sudhīra ring raṇa*

kapwâpakṣa manambut āyudha muwah saha sahana manunggang ing ratha,
sang hyang Śakra matanggu-tangguh amatūtakĕn apitutur ing patunggalan,
nāhan kāraṇa sang watĕk ratu paḍâmituturi sawarah sureśwara,
ramyârok wĕkasan tuhun hana wirang nira sahana watĕk Mahīsuta*

<Bhadralalita>:113.
⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓

ri tĕlas watĕk ratu paḍâhurip sukha narendra Krĕṣṇa magirang,
kadi ring pangipyan ika rakwa panghiḍĕp irêrikang mati kabeh,
paripūrṇa harṣa nira tulya warṣa paniram prapañca ri manah,
ndan ikā sukhê hati nira n tuminghal ing anak suputra salisu*

surarāja mamwit anĕhĕr mulih sira n umūr tĕkeng surapada,
awiwākṣitan sira kunang pwa sang ratu kabeh sirêki caritan,
naranātha Krĕṣṇa sira gorawâsĕgĕh i sang watĕk Kṣitisuta,
pinakaswabhāwa nira sang mahāpuruṣa toyarekha n agĕlĕng*

nrĕpa Cedi Karṇa Magadhendra Śālya pinakādi sampun arĕpat,
ubhaya n pinintakasihan mareng pura narendra Krĕṣṇa sakarĕng,
Yadu-Wrĕṣṇinātha nrĕpa Śālya len Drupada Bāhlikādi mapupul,
maśilā samâdulur i sang narendra Harimūrti tan hana waneh*

Basudewa Kimpuruṣanātha tan sipi girang nira n marajaya,
sĕmu ning lihat ciha-ciha n tuminghal i narendra Cedi maparĕk,
upacāra sambhrama nirâkadang pahula yan tĕlas parabhawa,
paḍa lampah ing hati wiwal kinubdha nira lokikêniring ira*

<Mrĕdukomala>:114.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓

mantuk sang naranātha Krĕṣṇa madulur lawan para ratu,
rājyêng Dwārawatī tinaṇḍas ira tan karânghinak-inak,
tan warṇan sira ring hĕnū mwang ikanang balâjĕmur arok,
āpan tulya pasang surud laku nira n sakeng pabharatan*

mangkā ng parwata ratna ramya mahawan tawang mibĕr alon,
lāwan sang Garuḍâdulur milu Sudarśanânghiringakĕn,
līlâsong jaladânipis kakĕñaran maṇīndra sumĕnö,
tumrang teja nikâwilĕt-wilĕt awor haneng jaladhara*

<Jagaddhita>:115.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏑| – ⏑ –| ⏑ ⏓

ndah warṇan gati ning balâlara ri mitra nika pĕjah anūtakĕn tuhan,
lāwan wāhw anilunglungî kadang ikā nĕhĕr angusapi luhnya tan pĕgat,
len tang māti kakā nikāna paḍa kāsrĕpan amĕkasi luh lawan sĕrĕh,
kapwâsong prihatin ry ulihnya hana kāry amuri-muri tangisnya tan humūng*

<Mrĕdukomala>:116.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ ⏓

strī belā kapapag mangiṣṭy akalihan sinuṇḍang awĕnĕs,
ceṭinyânangis ing wurinya pilih amwang amrih amalar,
tan sengĕh tinuhan-tuhan pijĕr asambat ing priya nikā,
lingnyânghing kaka her nghulun wuwus ikā n sumĕngka tumurun*

len manghĕmban anaknya patrĕm inagöm nikā n saha sĕrĕh,
tan pahyas gĕlungan mure tapih ikā banantĕn alĕsĕh,
marmâmakpak anak nikâmalaku suswanârdha kasatan,
tan trĕṣṇê wĕka kepwan anghangĕn-angĕn sĕnĕngnya kasihan*

tangheh yañ caritan laranya tucapêka sang prabhu kabeh,
prāptêng Dwārawatī sĕḍĕng pinaripoṣitêng sukha sira,
sakweh ning surabhogabhāra panamuy bhinukti surasa,
astam tang maṇi rājayogya sama yogya ring kadi sira*

sang Cedi mwang Awangganātha Magadhendra Śālya caritan,
manggĕh mitra kadang narendra Harimūrti ramya wĕkasan,
āpan tan mapuji ñ jayā nrĕpati Krĕṣṇa hetu ning asih,
sampun tuṣṭa kabeh tĕkeng balasahāya wastra masalin*

rwā ng we rwā ng wĕngi yan winurṣita mulih mareng swanagara,
sakweh sang pininang muwah sira mulih kabeh paḍa sukha,
hetunya n paripūrṇa kīrti nira nātha Krĕṣṇa mapagĕh,
pinras ring kajanapriyan tuwi pangöban ing sabhuwana*

<Wiśwalalita>:117.
⏑ ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑ ⏑| ⏑ – ⏑| – ⏑⏑| ⏑ ⏓

aparimitêng sukhâsama-samêng watĕk Yadu kabeh,
manginum agoṣṭhy amukti phala ning jayêng raṇasabhā,
irika narendra Krĕṣṇa Baladewa Pārtha manitah,
ri sĕnaha sang prawīra ginuṇêng tĕgal dinĕmakan*

sira para rājaputra dinadar dĕmak nira kabeh,
makawiṣayêrikang wiṣaya ning musuh tĕlas alah,
sama-sama sewu kāṭi nira sowang ing sawiṣaya,
ulih ing atoh ri jīwita nirâmrih ing pabharatan*

<Śārdūlawikrīḍita>:118.
– – –| ⏑ ⏑ – | ⏑ – ⏑| ⏑ ⏑ –| – – ⏑| – – ⏑| ⏓ 

sang nāthātmaja Sāmba sampun arĕṇah tekang dĕmak de haji,
an Prāgjyotiṣa rakwa punpunan ira ndātan hanânĕmpila,
mās rwang lakṣa kaṭi n kapangguhan irângkĕn māsa lek nohanĕn,
hīnganya n kalĕwih phala śrama nirâsārêng raṇâtoh bhaya*

sang nātha Druma mantuk ing swanagarêmbuh wanwa ring Yāwana,
bĕngkat-bĕngkat irâhawan ratha mure rambut nirêkâputih,
yapwan putra nirêka sang Suratha kāly âpan wineh putrikā,
de śrī Krĕṣṇa tĕlas paḍâsilih-asih rāgapriyânggöng smara*

ry antuk sang Garuḍâdulur sira lawan sang Pañcajanyânglayang,
mwang sang Komudikī Sudarśaṇa parĕng mwang Nandakânrang kilat,
prāptêng Wiṣṇupada ndatīta ta kabeh sang nātha Krĕṣṇâjarĕn,
sākṣāt wīrya nira n prakāśa karĕngö ring dik-widik niścala*

nāhan hetu ning aśwamedha ginawe ring Dwārawaty âdhika,
de sang śrī Basudewa kaprakaśitêng rāt mwang watĕk dewatā,
söh tang ratna suwarṇa ratnawanitā n panggorawêng brāhmaṇa,
mangdadyakĕna haywan ing bhuwana sākṣāt rîndralokânurun*

strī kanyâhayu ratnarājaduhitânwam pat hajöngyânulus,
antuk ning mamarājaya nrĕpati Krĕṣṇâmukti tātan waneh,
ramyâwarṇa tinunggal ing jinĕm arūm harṣa n saraśmîng tilĕm,
āpan de ni kawiṣṇumūrtin ira sang nātha n wĕnang wyāpaka*

ndan sang śrī warawīrya Rukma Krĕtadharmādi pralabdhêng sukha,
kapwâmukti sakāpti ning manah anūt dharmâpagĕh ring hayu,
swasthā ning bala ramya tan hana sasar sangkêrikang śāsana,
āstām sang caturāśramâtata manūt śāstrâhawan ring pada*
